###############################################################
### Testing ####
################
defined_text = {
	name = test_meta_loc
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU001
		}
		localization_key = focus_EU002
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001 }
		}
		localization_key = focus_EU003
	}
}


###############################################################
defined_text = {
	name = EU_parliament_Supermajority
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = european_constitution
				has_global_flag = european_federation
			}
		}
		localization_key = EU_parliament_Supermajority_loc_key
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = EU_parliament_political_groups
	text = {
		trigger = {
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.EU_member
				has_idea = EU_member
			}
		}
		localization_key = EU_parliament_political_groups_loc_key
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = EU_parliament_PG_Western_Autocracy_icon
	text = {
		trigger = {
			date < 2017.1.1
		}
		localization_key = EU_parliament_PG_Western_Autocracy_icon_loc_key
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			date > 2017.1.1
		}
		localization_key = EU_parliament_PG_2017_Western_Autocracy_icon_loc_key
	}
}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			BLR = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = EU_parliament_IND_Communist-State
				}
			}
			check_variable = { BLR.MEP_Communist-State > 0 }
		}
		localization_key = BLR_Communist-State_loc_key
	}
}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			LAT = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = EU_parliament_IND_Conservative
				}
			}
			check_variable = { LAT.MEP_Conservative > 0 }
		}
		localization_key = LAT_Conservative_loc_key
	}
}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			POR = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = EU_parliament_IND_Neutral_Autocracy
				}
			}
			check_variable = { POR.MEP_Neutral_Autocracy > 0 }
		}
		localization_key = POR_Neutral_Autocracy_loc_key
	}
}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			MLT = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = EU_parliament_IND_Monarchist
				}
			}
			check_variable = { MLT.MEP_Monarchist > 0 }
		}
		localization_key = MLT_Monarchist_loc_key
	}
}

############################
### EU Parliament Agenda ###
############################



defined_text = {
	name = EU_parliament_agenda
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					focus_EU001_draft = yes
					NOT = {
						focus_EU001_accepted = yes
					}
					NOT = {
						focus_EU001_EP_approval = yes
					}
				}

### Agenda focus loc ###

### EU001 ###

defined_text = {
	name = EU_parliament_focus_EU001
	text = {
		trigger = {
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.EU_member
				has_country_flag = focus_EU001_EP_agenda
			}
			focus_EU001_draft = yes
			NOT = {
				focus_EU001_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = {
				focus_EU001_EP_approval = yes
			}
		}
		localization_key = EU_parliament_focus_EU001_loc_key
	}
}
